Function: "StrSlash"
Exch($R3,0)
Exch(st(1),0)
Exch($R1,0)
Push: $R2
Push: $R4
Push: $R6
Push: $R7
StrCpy $R2 "" () ()
StrLen $R6 "$R1"
StrCpy $R4 "\" () ()
StrCmp "$R3" "/" equal=loop, nonequal=
StrCpy $R4 "/" () ()
StrCpy $R7 "$R1" (1) ()
StrCpy $R1 "$R1" ($R6) (1)
StrCmp "$R7" "$R3" equal=found, nonequal=
StrCpy $R2 "$R2$R7" () ()
StrCmp "$R1" "" equal=done, nonequal=loop
StrCpy $R2 "$R2$R4" () ()
StrCmp "$R1" "" equal=done, nonequal=loop
StrCpy $R3 "$R2" () ()
Pop: $R7
Pop: $R6
Pop: $R4
Pop: $R2
Pop: $R1
Exch($R3,0)
FunctionEnd
